 In his last address to the nation, President Pranab Mukherjee said that the Constitution had been like a holy book for him and the Parliament Temple

 Actually these are paintings hanging on the wall
 yah talaghar asal main must art gailaree kaa thikaana he
 Generally, the exhibition of traditional art of Gond tribesmen of Central India is organized here
 gond zyaadaatar madhya pradesh or chhattisgarh main rahete hai
 They have decorated the walls of village houses with such paintings

 isse bachane ke liye ham aapke liye lekar aae hai kuch jaruri tips-1
 Only when the lock symbol is displayed on the url login
 While doing online banking, always keep in mind that the lock (mostly in red) symbol on the url (url) of the website on which the site has the ID and password of your bank account
 Are visible is lock se pataa chalata he kipassword gopneey rakhaa jayega
 It is also indicative of the security of the website
 2
 Beware of fake email When a fraud person or organization sends fake email to you, it is called phishing
 aise i-mail main aapkaa bank acount number,password aadi jaanane kii koshish kii jaati he
 Never forget to click on the links given in it
 3
 Be sure to logout, no matter after you are in a hurry, never forget to logout your account on the Internet
 aapaki is choti si bhul se aapako bada nuksaan jhelana pad saktaa he
 4
 ghapala hone par bank ko turant den jaankarbgar aapke bank acount se paise nikaale gaye hai yaa kisi bhi tarah kaa koi ghapala hua he to isaki jaankaree bank ko turant den
 Also change the password as well
 vaise kuch dinon main password badalte rahanaa suraksha ko badhaata he

 In the Lok Sabha on Thursday, there was a fierce debate between Union Law Minister Ravi Shankar Prasad and AIMIM MP Asaduddin Owaisi regarding the Aadhaar bill
 is dauraan aadhaar bill par loksabhaa main charchaa karte hue ovaisi ne kaha ki yah sarkaar jeeyo or jeene do main nahin, balki sirf jeeyo-jeeyo-jeeyo main vishwaas karti he
 Addressing Ravi Shankar Prasad, he said, 'you take it in sarcasm
 aapako dekhakar aisa lag rahaa ki aap meraa encounter kar denge
 In response, Ravi Shankar Prasad said, 'we also take your satire seriously
 ' is ovaisi ne palatwaar karte hue kaha, 'aapkaa cheharaa bataa rahaa ki aap mujhe kha jaaenge
 The Aadhaar bill is unconstitutional
 aap loksabhaa main bhale hi is bill ko paarit kara len, lekin supreme court ke aage yah tik nahin paaegaa
 Owaisi said, "many provisions of this bill violate the orders of the Supreme Court
" yah halaala kaa clasik udhaaharan he, kyonki supreme court kah chukaa ki sarkari data privet companiyon ko nahin diya ja saktaa
 This has broken the marriage between the government and private companies and has become a classic case of Hallala
 ' ovaisi ne kaha ki sarkaar privet companiyon ke ishaaron par naach rahi he or use niztaa kii suraksha kii koi chintaa nahin he
 It is the same way that you took an electoral bond before an election from someone who made you a James Bond after the election
 kendriya kanoon mantri ravishankar prasad ne kaha, 'kuch saansad kah rahe hai ki ham supreme court ke faisle ke khilaaf kyon ja rahe hai? main kahata hum ki loksabhaa ko kanoon banane kaa adhikaar he

 'aaj aadhaar ke jariye manaregaa ke labhaarthiyon ke khate main sidhe paise bheje ja rahe hai

 this is not right
